POKEMON GEN 1-3 ENRICHMENT
FULL GEN 3 LEARNSETS FORMAT
Based on the user's uploaded National Dex catalog (#001-#386)

==============================================================================


==============================================================================
V18 MINIMAL LEVEL-UP OVERLAP NOTES
==============================================================================

This pass keeps broad egg-move overlap, but cuts level-up overlap down sharply.

Design rules for this pass:
- Egg move additions are retained as the main expansion path.
- Level-up support remains available, but only as a very small overlap bridge.
- Level-up support is reduced to a short curated subset per edited line.
- Preference is given to STAB reinforcement, one signature utility option, and
  one reasonable accessibility bridge where needed.
- Original learnsets and expanded egg sections are otherwise preserved.


==============================================================================
V14 BREEDING-FIRST LEARNSET / EGG MOVE EXPANSION NOTES
==============================================================================

This pass shifts the aggressive overhaul to a breeding-first model.

Design rules for this pass:
- Every species was reviewed again with level-up additions minimized.
- Egg move pools were expanded even more aggressively than before.
- Breeding access was treated as the preferred delivery method for new move access.
- The full expanded move catalog was treated as available distribution material.
- New additions were filtered to avoid repeating moves already present in each species entry.
- Priority was given to STAB identity, weak-type support, broader line viability, and breeding accessibility.

Practical result:
- Every species received a breeding-first learnset review.
- Every species received a very large egg move expansion section.
- The expanded move pool is now pushed toward egg access wherever possible, with level-up additions kept lean.

==============================================================================
V16 BREEDING LEGALITY SUPPORT NOTES
==============================================================================

This pass keeps the breeding-first philosophy, but fixes the legality issue that
expanded egg moves need father-accessible sources.

Design rules for this pass:
- Level-up additions remain minimized.
- Expanded egg moves are retained where appropriate.
- Each expanded egg move is also mirrored into TM access on the same line as a
  practical breeding-support source for male parents and same-line chaining.
- This is an implementation-first legality patch, not a competitive rebalance.
- No original learnset content was removed by this pass.

==============================================================================
V10 REDISTRIBUTION PASS NOTES
==============================================================================

This pass focused on redistributing existing BST more intelligently instead of primarily raising or lowering totals.

Redistribution targets
- Blastoise: shifted toward slower mixed bulk/tank identity for Water / Ground
- Raichu: reduced pure speed skew and added sturdier Electric / Steel profile
- Donphan: pushed harder into physical wall / bruiser stats
- Sceptile: redistributed into a more balanced fast mixed Dragon-style attacker
- Milotic: reduced excess speed and improved bulky special dragon identity
- Paras / Parasect: reinforced slow disruptive Bug / Ghost stat lines with more special bulk
- Hoothoot / Noctowl: better matched Fire / Psychic special attacker / utility roles
- Spinarak / Ariados: smoothed awkward stat lines into clearer ambush bruiser roles
- Sunkern: kept weak but gave it a cleaner special growth profile
- Jigglypuff / Wigglytuff: reduced awkward stat waste and pushed clearer Psychic and Psychic / Fighting roles
- Delibird: moved away from over-reliance on Speed into a more functional offensive utility spread
- Luvdisc: lowered excessive speed concentration and improved special utility profile

This pass intentionally emphasized role definition over raw BST movement.

==============================================================================
V11 REDISTRIBUTION PASS NOTES
==============================================================================

This pass kept BST totals the same and focused only on cleaner role identity.

Updated redistribution targets:
- Blastoise: shifted toward slower mixed tank / shell-cannon bulk
- Raichu: reduced dead physical investment, cleaner Electric / Steel special role
- Jigglypuff: leaned harder into bulky Psychic disruption
- Wigglytuff: cleaned into a more physical Psychic / Fighting bruiser-support
- Noctowl: reduced dead Attack, stronger Fire / Psychic special utility profile
- Ariados: committed harder to physical ambush pressure, cut wasted SpA
- Sunflora: committed harder to sun-burst special offense
- Delibird: cleaned into faster special utility/offense
- Milotic: reduced dead Attack, reinforced bulky special wall identity
- Luvdisc: reduced dead Attack, cleaner fast special support profile

Design rule for this pass:
- Keep BST stable
- Reduce stat waste
- Sharpen role definition
- Avoid broad inflation
